To tame you'd still need the required amount of stamina\n- 5 Tames %3D +1 stamina restored\n- 10 Tames %3D +2 stamina restored\n- 20 Tames %3D +3 stamina restored\n- 40 Tames %3D +4 stamina restored \n\nNotes:\n- (for selling) Some fapets by default are pricier then others (usually if their taming procedure is more complex then the selling price would also be higher)=<align%3Dleft><size%3D25>要求：驯服点、配方、耐力点（查看 fapet 的配方）、任何与配方相关的物品/技能\n\n信息：驯服是一种特殊程序（利用 fapet 的恋物癖）来变野fapet 变成你自己的奴隶\n\n注意：\n- 如果驯服程序似乎不起作用，最好查看它的配方，检查任何细节\n- 如果你没有足够的耐力点驯服程序将导致失败，在某些情况下会导致失败\n- 一些 fapets 可能需要更多的耐力（并且总体上更具挑战性）才能成功驯服\n\n驯服专长：驯服后耐力部分恢复（例如：驯服 5 'th 兔子 3 耐力, 驯服后恢复 1). 恢复的耐力不能高于驯服所花费的。要驯服你仍然需要足够的耐力\n- 5 Tames %3D +1 耐力恢复\n- 10 Tames %3D +2 耐力恢复\n- 20 Tames %3D +3 耐力恢复\n- 40 驯服 %3D +4 耐力恢复 \n\n注意：\n-（用于出售）默认情况下，一些 fapets 比其他的更贵（通常如果它们的驯服程序更复杂，那么售价也会更高）

<align%3Dleft><size%3D25>Special actions which can be perfomed during an hAct. Primarily their funtion is to boost the partner's arrousment\nBasics:\n- h-actions are replacing quickslots, being shown at the bottom of the screen, they can be activated by holding pressed the according number key (on keyboard above letters QWERT) 1,2, etc. The one in left corner is Cancel/Stop [0 key], it'll cancel th hAct upon getting the appearing gauge filled. It's filling speed depends on character's arrousment, higher arr - slower filling speed.\nNot all hActs have h-actions. Forced and attacking hActs have no canceling\n\nNotes:\n- If one of them is displayed as locked, then it can probably be unlocked by having multiple hacts or increasing their h-experience=<align%3Dleft><size%3D25>可以在 hAct 期间执行的特殊操作。它们的主要作用是提高伙伴的热情\n基本：\n- h-actions正在取代quickslots，显示在屏幕底部，它们可以通过按住相应的数字键来激活（在键盘上的字母QWERT上方）1 ,2 等。左角的一个是取消/停止 [0 键]，它会在出现的仪表被填满时取消 hAct。它的填充速度取决于角色的热情，较高的 arr - 较慢的填充速度。\n并非所有 hAct 都有 h-actions。强制和攻击 hActs 没有取消\n\n注意：\n- 如果其中一个显示为锁定，那么它可能可以通过拥有多个 hacts 或增加他们的 h 经验来解锁

Some states affect the drain and replenish rate (ex: pregnant mode).\n\nNotes:\n- In some cases energy's cap can lower. It can only be restored by sleeping in comfort (in a house/room)=<align%3Dleft><size%3D25>能量用于使人筋疲力尽的活动，例如跑步、hAct 中的安慰或试图逃离 hAct。某些状态会影响消耗和补充速率（例如：怀孕模式）。\n\n注意：\n- 在某些情况下，能量上限会降低。它只能通过舒适地睡觉来恢复（在房子/房间里）

1. Crowd Chars with an indicator above their heads are interactable NPCs=1. 头顶有指示器的人群角色是可交互的 NPC
2. Indicator colors: Blueish - AvailableQuest, Gray - InProgress Quest, Green - Finished Quest, Orange - Shop=2. 指示灯颜色：蓝色 - AvailableQuest，灰色 - InProgress Quest，绿色 - 已完成任务，橙色 - 商店
3. Book: registers active quests (icon showing if it's in progress or finished), and on Select - Highlights the NPC in the world (look around for a blueish beam)=3. 书：登记活动任务（图标显示它是在进行中还是完成），在选择上 - 突出显示世界中的 NPC（四处寻找蓝色光束）
4. Tips: Interacting with the NPC will show the current progress and will Highlight the target's location (in some cases)=4. 提示：与NPC互动会显示当前进度并会突出显示目标的位置（在某些情况下）
